Female, 76 - 89 years

Age Reported Symptoms Notes
76 2021-01-06 feeling abnormal Developed a severe headache within 2-3 hours of receiving vaccine. Took 2 Tylenol. Headache abated b... Read more
Close
Developed a severe headache within 2-3 hours of receiving vaccine. Took 2 Tylenol. Headache abated but did not resolve. Within the next 2-3 hours felt tingling in my left upper lip. It grew worse and headache worsened. Lip felt like it was swelling but no change was seen. Then left side of face began to ache. Took 2 more Tylenol. Texted my primary care physician who recommended Benadryl in case it was an allergic reaction. Took Benadryl about 4:30 or 5:00. Left work and went home. Had severe headache. Took my blood pressure. It was 185/68. Had some old Propanolol 10 mg from 2 years earlier and took one and a Prednisone 10mg. By 9:00 pm still felt bad with facial pain and tingling. BP decreased to 148/89. Took another Benadryl and went to bed. Face ant lip better in the morning. Arm sore for 2 days. Developed body and joint aches for the past 2-3 days. Slowly resolving.
76 2021-01-08 feeling abnormal Pt c/o having 'weird feeling/not feeling good' and increase heart rate about 7-8 minutes after recei... Read more
Close
Pt c/o having 'weird feeling/not feeling good' and increase heart rate about 7-8 minutes after receiving vaccine. Pt denied any shortness of breath at the time, no swelling of face, BBS clear and equal with equal rise and fall of the chest wall, alert and oriented X 4, able to speak in complete sentences. Progressed to report 'lips feeling like they are swelling approximately 18 minutes after the vaccine was administered. 911 was activated. Epinephrine 0.3 mg IM via epi autoinjector was administered to left thigh. Pt still c/o feeling that her lips were swelling 8 minutes after first dose of Epinephrine; therefore, another dose of 0.3 mg Epinephrine IM via epi autoinjector was administered to left thigh. Diphenhydramine 25 mg IV was administered 2 minutes after second dose of Epinephrine. IV fluids administered as well, while awaiting arrive of EMS. EMS arrived on scene approximately 30 minutes after called. Blood glucose was 120 mg/dl approximately 25 minutes after vaccine administration. Pt report feeling better after the 2nd dose of Epinephrine and Diphendydramine and 500 ml of Normal saline IV. Pt was transported via EMS to the ER for further evaluation and treatment.

One week after receiving the vaccine shot, my left upper arm from should down began to itch. Slight red, under the skin 'rash' could barely be seen. The individual spots did not seem to be the specific irritant. The arm around the shoulder was somewhat achy and tight feeling. I was able to sleep through the night after rubbing on Sarno-anti itch lotion. Could not get comfortable on my left side, with the shoulder area hurting.

Received the second dose of Moderna on Friday afternoon at 3 p.m., Awakened in the middle of the night with significant muscle pain. Unable to sleep. Was unable to stay awake on Saturday. Slept almost all day. I took no medication. Did not seek medical care. Used my Series E Apple watch to monitor my heart rate: 80 bpm average. Side effects were gone by the next day, Sunday.

76 2021-01-26 loss of personal independence in daily activities 1/9/21 At 3:50 am started with nausea, weakness, and complaints of body aches. Required more assista... Read more
Close
1/9/21 At 3:50 am started with nausea, weakness, and complaints of body aches. Required more assistance with ADL's than previous. @ 4:28 am: complaints of SOB, O2 sats 85% on room air. Required supplement O2, with tremors noted. PRN Zofran administered for nausea. 7:42 am noted with fever, decreased O2 sats, Tylenol administered for fever. Fever continue to climb despite Tylenol, supplemental O2 increased to 4L, rapid covid test negative, new orders to start Rocephin IM x 3 days and stat Xray which showed pneumonia. Temperature continues to remain elevated- O2 status continues to decline. Sent to ER 1/9/2021 @ 4:53 pm via ambulance. Admitted to Hospital with ABT tx for pneumonia and UTI. Respiratory status continued to decline- pulmonology consulted- Placed in ICU 1/13/21 and started on steroids. Required BiPap and was eventually weaned to supplemental O2. Multiple Covid tests- all negative. GI complaints addressed with GI consult- unremarkable. Started on PPI and Linzess. Eventually was placed on telemetry floor, closely monitored by pulmonology, and was cleared for discharge on 1/19/2021 back to nursing home.

On 1-23-21, left arm became sore area of injection site; hurt to lie on left side to sleep. On 1-24-21, in am, upper arm very sore and red area, 3? X 1 1/2? at site. By evening it was more red and sore. Morning of 1-25-21, red area was more diffuse. Same evening, redness started to fade in center, creating a ?figure 8? appearance, with faded area in centers of figure 8 circles. Morning of 1-26-21, redness nearly gone, much less soreness. Today, 1-27-21, no redness but arm slightly sore to touch. Note, arm was sore for only three days after vaccination given.

76 2021-01-29 sleep disorder Began to have slight wheezing and coughing on Wed afternoon, the day after getting the shot. Thursd... Read more
Close
Began to have slight wheezing and coughing on Wed afternoon, the day after getting the shot. Thursday wheezing and coughing increased and woke me up during the night several times. Cough was productive with clear sputum. Friday felt very tired all day and coughing and wheezing increased substantially, producing shortness of breath upon any exertion, like going up and down the stairs. Very tired. Began to think I'd have to go to see the Dr. because wheezing was significant with every breath. Cough was racking, increasing through the day into the evening. At 10 p.m. I began to wonder if I'd make it through the night without calling the rescue squad. Couldn't take a deep breath or speak a whole sentence with out a coughing jag. Then, suddenly about 11:30, it just ceased. The tightness in my chest went away, the coughing with every inhalation stopped and I could take a deep breath. It was a bit stunning. Because I had pulmonary embollisms about ten years ago, my lungs have been a weak spot in my body with bronchitis occurring frequently. I hadn't seen reports of this side effect of the vaccine, so I thought I'd report it. This morning, Saturday four days after the shot, I am breathing much better, not coughing, and do not have any wheezing.

76 2021-02-04 feeling abnormal Afib; Feeling uncomfortable; Blood sugar was around 150, which is higher than her normal levels; A s... Read more
Close
Afib; Feeling uncomfortable; Blood sugar was around 150, which is higher than her normal levels; A spontaneous report was received from a consumer who is 76-year-old, female patient, who received Moderna's COVID-19 Vaccine (mRNA-1273) and experienced atrial fibrillation, feeling uncomfortable, and increased blood sugar. The patient's medical history included diabetes and atrial fibrillation. Concomitant medications were not reported. On 02 Jan 2021, the patient received their first two planned doses of mRNA-1273 (Batch number: 025LZ0A) intramuscularly in her right arm for the prophylaxis of COVID-19 infection. On 02 Jan 2021, the patient experienced heart beating very fast and feeling uncomfortable; it lasted for a few hours. She stated it was atrial fibrillation, she had a diagnosis of this, and it only lasted a few hours. The patient also stated that her blood glucose was 150, which was higher than normal. Treatment for the events was not provided. Action taken with mRNA-1273 in response to the events was not reported. The outcome of events, increased blood sugar, was considered not resolved. The outcome of the events, atrial fibrillation and feeling uncomfortable, was considered resolved.; Reporter's Comments: This case concerns a 76 year-old female patient with a significant medical history of atrial fibrillation and diabetes, who experienced a serious unexpected event of Atrial fibrillation and non-serious unexpected events of Discomfort and Blood glucose increased. The events occurred one day (same day) after first dose of mRNA-1273, lot # 025LZ0A. Treatment was not reported. Based on the current available information and temporal association between the use of the product and onset of the event a causal relationship cannot be excluded. However, patient's medical history of atrial fibrillation and diabetes were considered strong confounders.

76 2021-02-27 incoherent Almost exactly 24 hours after 2nd shot, my mom was getting her hair done and she started breathing h... Read more

Almost exactly 24 hours after 2nd shot, my mom was getting her hair done and she started breathing hard. Hairstylist removed her mask and she then passed out. Called 911. They observed my mom sweating, her lips and hands were swollen, she was slack jawed, pale and clammy. After several minutes she came out of it. Was given a piece of candy thinking it was a sugar low, but her sugar was high 285 @9:00am. Her color was still pale and she was still incoherent. While still on with 911, she became more lucid and said she was feeling better, so ambulance was canceled. I drove her home and checked her sugar @11:00 - 295 and BP 125/55 pulse 75. She stayed with me for the rest of Saturday. Her sugar was still high Saturday evening and Sunday morning. Upon checking her blood sugar log, her sugar had gone up for a week following the first shot.
76 2021-02-28 insomnia Periodic pressure and tightness across chest and diaphragm especially on day of vaccination and fol... Read more
Close
Periodic pressure and tightness across chest and diaphragm especially on day of vaccination and following 2 days. Rapid heart beat followed by afib that was not terminated with normal medications. Dizziness and shortness of breath. Hospitalized with atrial fibrillation with rapid ventricular response. It resolved after getting two injections of a medication called diltiazem in the emergency department, after which I was monitored overnight in the hospital. Underwent stress test and echocardiogram - results normal. On the day I write this (March 1) continue to have shorter periods of rise in blood pressure and heart rate, diaphragm tightness, insomnia and lethargy.

Second dose of vaccine, Lot# 013A21A, was administered on 3/5/2021 at 10:52AM to the left deltoid. Approximately 5 minutes after receiving second dose, patient reported feeling anxious and feeling like her blood pressure was increasing. Patient taken to EMS observation area. Patient with flushing. No generalized hives. No itching. No swelling of face, lips, or eyes. Left deltoid injection site without erythema or swelling. Skin warm and dry. Lungs auscultated and inspiratory wheeze noted in all lung fields. No shortness of breath. No cough. No nasal congestion. No change in voice. No sensation of throat closing. No stridor. I am starting this report with the current status of my, nearly, 6-week ordeal of agonizing pain, doctor appts. debilitation, pain meds, a blood test and the final MRI this past Saturday, 3/6. Finally, an MRI has confirmed physician's recent suspicion that my second Moderna vaccination was improperly administered. In fact, it tore a tendon in my right shoulder. I knew something was wrong when I saw how high the needle was injected into my arm/shoulder. I just didn't know what the ramifications would be. I have been referred to a surgeon, and my appt. is 3/16). Summary of Events: On 2/1/21, I received my second dose of the Moderna vaccine and had 2 days of moderate pain and soreness. But about 3 days later, 2/4, I awoke to excruciating shoulder/arm pain that had me sobbing out loud. I took Tylenol and waited. Nothing. I took more Tylenol and slowly the pain diminished. For an hour or so. All I could do was lie on the couch, literally, groaning and unable to lift my arm By evening, the only relief I could get was from an old (hip surgery) Oxycodone pill. I took 1/4 piece and slept the night. Friday and Saturday I was totally debilitated. I couldn't lift my arm, care for my dog or do anything but lie on the couch, still sobbing, until small pieces of the Oxy set in again. It was the weekend, and I didn't want to bother anyone but I never felt such pain for such an extended time or survived so long on meds. Monday morning, 2/8/21, I called my Doctor. I was very concerned and really wanted to make sure this pain was still from the vaccine and not some "weird" condition that might have hit me. The office told me the pain was probably from the vaccine and advised me to keep taking Tylenol. So it continued, on and off, relief and agony. I was sure it would stop. It didn't. Thursday, 2/11, I saw the Doctor, in person. Physician did not have an answer for the pain but gave me a prescription for Celebrex and did a blood test to see if there was a bacteria infection that might have invaded the area. We would wait for results. Another weekend of pain but lessened a bit. Around 2/13, a neighbor called me with an article he found about the SAME situation MANY people were suffering (thousands) and LAWSUITS pending!! I didn't know what was happening to me but the Gov't did. The article was found on internet, 2/12, and printed an article from news paper, 2/12 No other reports appeared anywhere. The pertinent findings of the article: thousands of vaccinated people (Covid and flu) have reported similar pain and debilitation. The previous gov't has introduced a law prohibiting lawsuits (l think against the pharmas but not the administering agencies. Not sure.) that was to go into effect, 2/23. Again, not sure of details. But no one knows about this - people NEED to know. I immediately notified my family and close friend about my situation. While the cause is not certain, it is suspected that improper injection technique/training/experience is to blame. To get the word out, I posted on social media, wrote representatives, etc. And now I found you. The information must be made available; not to stop vaccinations but to alert the public if they occur.

On 10-Mar-2021, received second dose of mRNA-1273 (Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine) (Intramuscular) dosage was changed to 1 dosage form. The patient was treated with Surgery (On 18-may-2021, patient underwent intestinal surgery to remove diseased section.) for Diverticulitis. On 12-Mar-2021, HEADACHE (Splitting headache) and MYALGIA (Body aches/ Achy flu system) had resolved. At the time of the report, DIVERTICULITIS (Stomach pain which ended in diverticulitis attack), PAIN IN EXTREMITY (Right arm tender) and ABDOMINAL PAIN UPPER (Stomach pain which ended in diverticulitis attack) had not resolved, VACCINATION SITE REACTION (COVID arm), FEELING ABNORMAL (Doesn't felt great), NASOPHARYNGITIS (Cold), HYPERHIDROSIS (Sweating), CHILLS (Chills) and NAUSEA (Nausea) outcome was unknown, INFLUENZA LIKE ILLNESS (COVID Flu Symptoms) had resolved with sequelae and PYREXIA (Fever) had resolved. DIAGNOSTIC RESULTS (normal ranges are provided in parenthesis if available): On 10-Mar-2021, Body temperature: increased (High) increased. No concomitant medications were reported. Patient reported to have no health issues for the past 18 months, before administration of mRNA-1273. Very limited information regarding this events has been provided at this time. Activated a BAKERS SYSTS; she could not get up, she could not go to bathroom; Left leg was very sore; Left leg very swollen; Chills; Had fever; Inconsistencies to remember; Not feel well; Delirious; A spontaneous report was received from a consumer concerning 88-years-old, female patient, who received Moderna's COVID-19 vaccine (mRNA-1273) and experienced bad reaction, began to not feel well, had fever, was delirious, inconsistencies with speech, problems with the left leg, left leg was very sore, very swollen, could not get up, had chills, couldn't sit in the bathroom, overreaction and activated a Baker's cyst The patient's medical history was not provided. No relevant concomitant medications were reported. On 16 Feb 2021, approximately three hours prior to the onset of the events, the patient received their second of two planned doses of mRNA-1273 (Batch Number 032L20A) intramuscularly in the left arm for prophylaxis of COVID-19 infection. On 16 Feb 2021, the patient experienced to not feel well, had fever, was delirious(considered medically significant event), inconsistencies to remember, problems with the left leg. On Wednesday 17 Feb 2021, the patient experienced left leg was very sore, very swollen, could not get up, could not go to the bathroom, had a fever and chills. On Thursday 18 Feb 2021, the patient experienced could not sit in the bathroom. On Friday 19 Feb 2021, the patient was still very swollen. On an unknown date, the patient experienced activated a BAKERS SYSTS Laboratory details included, on Saturday 20 Feb 2021, the patient went to the hospital and got an ECO DOPPLER. Treatment for the event included Ibuprofen. Action taken with mRNA-1273 in response to the events was not reported. The outcome of the events, bad reaction, began to not feel well, she had a fever, she was delirious, said inconsistencies, problems with the left leg, left leg was very sore, very swollen, could not get up, could not go to the bathroom, had a fever and chills, couldn't sit in the bathroom, overreaction and activated a BAKERS SYSTS was considered recovering(getting better every day).; Reporter's Comments: Based on the current available information and a temporal association between the use of the product and the start date of the event and excluding all other etiologies, a causal relationship cannot be excluded.

Close
began seeing hallucinations; A spontaneous report was received from a consumer concerning a 89-year-old, female patient, who received Moderna's COVID-19 vaccine (mRNA-1273) and began seeing hallucinations. The patient's medical history was not provided. No relevant concomitant medications were reported. On 01 Feb 2021, about 4 hours prior to the onset of the event, the patient received their first of two planned doses of mRNA-1273 (Lot number: 013M20A) intramuscularly in the right arm for prophylaxis of COVID-19 infection. On 01 Feb 2021, about 4 hours after receiving the vaccine, the patient began seeing hallucinations. She was seeing moss grow on the walls and real bright turquoise colors that turn pink. No treatment information was provided. Action taken with mRNA-1273 in response to the event was not reported. The outcome of the event began seeing hallucinations was unknown.; Reporter's Comments: This case concerns a 89 year-old, female patient, who experienced event of hallucinations. The event occurred 4 hours after the first and last dose of mRNA-1273 vaccine administration. Based on the current available information and temporal association between the use of the product and the start date of the event, a causal relationship cannot be excluded and the event is assessed as possibly related.

89 2021-03-07 memory impairment, hallucination, amnesia My mother has experienced a severe reaction to her vaccine. Diagnosed with brain encephalopathy prob... Read more
Close
My mother has experienced a severe reaction to her vaccine. Diagnosed with brain encephalopathy probably caused by molecular mimicry in response to the Covid vaccine, she is now being treated as an inpatient at the Clinic. She was fully independent- living alone, mobile, with excellent cognitive function. On January 21, 2021 she received her 1st Moderna vaccine. Subsequently family noticed small balance changes, slight fine motor coordination changes (handwriting, etc) and a little forgetfulness not previously seen. Everything was chalked up to her being 89 years old. She remained independent and relatively fully functional. Patient is now unable to stand without assistance, leans backward when trying to stand, has developed a spastic tremor bilaterally in her arms, and her cognition is completely altered. Hallucinations, memory loss, can follow some directions but not all, speech clear but inappropriate. This declines DAILY. As of March 7th, she could not identify immediate family members in a photo. These changes have all occurred within the past few weeks and appear to have an acute underlying cause not related to age. Medical staff are looking at an autoimmune encephalitis picture based on the antibodies developed from the vaccine attacking the tissue in the brain and spinal cord that resembles the small piece of the vaccine. She is currently at the Clinic affiliated hospital. At this time, family is contacting Clinic main campus to request further investigation. Photographic evidence of rapid decline available, but not able to attach to this form: Available are three pictures of a log patient keeps with her vitals that she was doing every day. 1. Personal log of vital signs pre Covid vaccine/dose 1 - you can see the handwriting is concise, clear, and orderly. 2. Personal log of vitals after Covid dose 1 on Jan. 21 - slight changes in the handwriting and orderliness but still ok. 3. Personal log of vitals after Covid vaccine dose 2 Feb. 17 - note the illegible handwriting, missing entries, and no spatial awareness of line alignment. Available are three photos of crossword puzzles she does every day. 1. Puzzle dated Feb.12. Demonstrates her ability to accurately fill most answers with clear writing. 2. Puzzle dated Feb.19 shows an ability to fill in only a couple answers with obvious handwriting changes. 3. Puzzle dated Feb. 21 shows inability to complete, and a strange discrepancy between ability and inability- note 29 across and 18 down. Patients outcome is undetermined as diagnosis/treatment and prognosis are ongoing.

89 2021-04-01 confusional state, mental status changes Patient received her second coronavirus vaccination on March 18, 2021. Shortly thereafter she becam... Read more
Close
Patient received her second coronavirus vaccination on March 18, 2021. Shortly thereafter she became confused. Patient developed anorexia and weakness after the second coronavirus vaccination. Patient presented to the emergency department 3/21/21 with confusion and hyponatremia and was discharged home. She represented to ED on 3/24/21 for altered mental status and was admitted with encephalopathy and hyponatremia after several days of confusion. Patient required Haldol as well as lorazepam and received 3% saline. She had an MRI of the brain showing no acute intracranial process and radiograph of the chest showing no acute findings. She was discharged home 3/26/21 but then returned to the ED 3/29/21 for altered mental status, confusion and dehydration and was admitted with toxic metabolic encephalopathy. MD feels toxic metabolic encephalopathy related to second coronavirus vaccination.
